## SYSTEM CRASHES (BSODs, UNEXPECTED REBOOTS)

- **Blue Screen crashes (BSOD):** 0
- **Unexpected reboots:** 2
- **Crash dump files:** 0

**Reboot causes:**

- Unexpected power loss / hard reboot: 2

Timing proximity: 1 of 2 unexpected reboots landed within
5 minutes of an nvlddmkm GPU error. Treat as a timing hint, not a cause — a
5-minute window will catch some coincidences on systems with many of either.

**Crash timeline:**

```
    2026-05-15 10:04:57  [REBOOT]  Unexpected reboot: Unexpected power loss / hard reboot (code 0x00000000)
```

## LIVE KERNEL DUMP ANALYSIS

_No new LiveKernel dumps copied from system folder this run; any dump(s) below were staged by an earlier run._

Live kernel dumps are non-BSOD kernel dumps Windows captures when a recoverable or attempted-recovery kernel fault occurs. GPU hangs often appear here without a matching nvlddmkm 13/14/153 event and without a WER application crash. Treat these as primary diagnostic evidence for the "no event log spam, no BSOD, but something hung" case.

Source folder: `C:\Windows\LiveKernelReports`
Scanned: 25 dump(s) within last 6 day(s)
Orphans: 1 cached analysis/-es for dumps whose source `.dmp` has been removed (rendered below).
Deep analysis (cdb): enabled (`%USERPROFILE%\AppData\Local\Microsoft\WindowsApps\cdbx64.exe`)
